## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: population ecology / mathematical biology (population dynamics ODEs)
**Analysis**: The target dP_dt is an instantaneous population growth rate driven by current population size P and possibly explicit time-dependence t (e.g., seasonality, interventions). This matches classical population dynamics models formulated as differential equations dP_dt = f(t, P) with mechanisms like density dependence, Allee effects, harvesting, and time-varying carrying capacity.

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Exponential (Malthusian) growth ODE: dP_dt = c0 * P (constant per-capita growth rate, low-density regime)
- Time-dependent per-capita rate: dP_dt = (c0 + c1 * t) * P (slow trend in environment or demography)
- Seasonally forced per-capita rate: dP_dt = (c0 + c1 * sin(c2 * t + c3)) * P (periodic environment/seasonality)
- Power-law (allometric) growth: dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 (nonlinear scaling of growth with population size)
- Density-dependent (Verhulst-type) growth ODE: dP_dt = c0 * P * (c1 - P) (self-limitation via crowding; carrying capacity embedded in c1)
- Generalized theta-logistic (Richards-type) ODE: dP_dt = c0 * P * (c1 - P**c2) (flexible density-dependence curvature)
- Gompertz growth ODE: dP_dt = c0 * P * log(c1 / P) (multiplicative growth with logarithmic density feedback)
- Allee effect (weak/strong) ODE: dP_dt = c0 * P * (P - c1) (low-density suppression; threshold at c1)
- Allee + carrying capacity: dP_dt = c0 * P * (P - c1) * (c2 - P) (growth negative at low P and above capacity)
- Linear harvesting/effort removal: dP_dt = c0 * P - c1 (constant-yield harvest or constant removal)
- Proportional harvesting/mortality: dP_dt = c0 * P - c1 * P (additional per-capita loss term)
- Time-varying carrying capacity (implicit): dP_dt = c0 * P * (c1 + c2 * sin(c3 * t) - P) (capacity oscillates with time)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope ŌåÆ Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects ŌåÆ Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay ŌåÆ Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior ŌåÆ Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects ŌåÆ Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Per-capita growth diagnosis: if dP_dt / P is approximately constant over P, favor dP_dt = c * P; if dP_dt / P varies with P, favor density-dependent terms.
- Crowding/self-limitation signature: dP_dt increases with P at small P but bends down at larger P; captured by a negative quadratic/cubic term in P (e.g., P*(c - P), P*(c - P**nu)).
- Carrying capacity interpretation: a stable equilibrium P* occurs where dP_dt = 0 and (Ōłé/ŌłéP) dP_dt at P* is negative; polynomial factorizations like P*(c1-P) make equilibria explicit.
- Allee effect signature: negative growth at low P with a positive growth region only after a threshold; captured by factors like P*(P-cA) or P*(P-cA)*(cK-P).
- Gompertz-type regulation cue: if per-capita growth dP_dt/P decreases roughly linearly with log(P), favor dP_dt = c * P * log(cK/P).
- Seasonality/intervention cue: if residuals vs t show periodicity after accounting for P-dependence, include sin(c*t + phi) modulation of parameters (e.g., growth rate or capacity).
- Harvesting/removal cue: if dP_dt remains negative even at moderate P or shows a near-constant downward shift, include a constant subtraction term (ŌłÆc) or extra mortality (ŌłÆc*P).
- Nonlinear scaling cue: if log(|dP_dt|) vs log(P) is approximately linear, a power-law dP_dt = c * P**alpha is plausible (often for aggregated or spatially structured populations).
